hath gretter pyte noble perſone men deſolate royaume then̄e ye haue ſelf therfore madame thēke ye theſe thīges beware cruelte defaure goode louer ād frēde hit pleſe fall deſpayre wote neuer may wordes 〈◊〉 ſtrōg nouh bete doun̄ ouercome conſtan̄ce cō tinen̄ce j loue men peple naturelly ende alle worlde knowe ſaye trouth alſo lōg al ſoule abideth body j ſhal neuer haue loue ne aliā ce vnto myn enmye ſpeke nomore therof king vainquiſſhid diſcōforted ſocours ſo terribly diſplaiſid angry aſpre mortal angre grete diſpair wāhope ſaide fell lady moſt rebell leſte pietoꝰ euer deꝑted womās bely ſyn j muſt acquite whā ꝑceyue ſwete corage wole accorde vnto ne entēde vnto cōtinuel ſupplicacions ſo trewe louer deporte hensforth ſpeke ony mater j yow ēſure ſone triews ſhall faille ye shalbe guerdoned yower fierſte ¶ theſe wordes kīg sklauonye departed thēs chiere pēſyf retourned ooſte deſiring come entēcion thā euer hadde bē ſore ſayr mirro lytil ſetting menace begā deuiſe ſōme gētil womē recoūtīg thē prayer requeſtes mortall enemy made ¶ ſhal ſaye yow triews faylled tyme ſette eſpired whā thꝰ faylled king ſclauonie thī king fayr mirro thā nede made men putte hē armes many daye▪ hoping oliferne ſholde come ād make ſkarmuches loſte payne ther ī cyte ony man durſte yſſue aſſayble thē aſmoche alway agaynſt hē worſe thā whā knewe oliferne ſo cremeuſe rebouted durſt come choſe ō daye fyfty knightes ſayde thē loue lady wold juſte agayn thē one aft ſyn brought hē vnto place ꝓpice juſte right fair ſighte theym cite begā thei iuſte making merueylloꝰ abruyt olyferne herde hit anō ran vnto vateillemēt lowpes walles iaſō wēte ſee theſe iouſtes anon ſawe maner sklauonoys grtee ſorou ſelf meruaillous corage went palas fore fayr mirro olyferne ſone iaſon reentr •• ſie wed mā woman childrē bleſſid ſayng one another neuer ſeen none lyk 〈◊〉 beaulte ne vaillyaunt knight body al cyte began • eyoye •• whan ſayr myrro thought iaſon vnarmed▪ ſhe ſente cam gladly al deſir whā comen fore ſale wed ſhe rendrid ſale ſyn demanded hym hou felte ſelf ferde certes madame āſ werde jaſon god begyue thā king ne fele body good diſpoſicion ād ioyouſly retorned cyte regarde enemyes haue felt thē thīketh ought fore dredde ne doubted ſhort tyme ye ſhall haue good rayſon haue day made ſwerd reed ī bloode wherof kīg mortel enemye hath grete dueyl ād ſoro haue yet goode wil morn̄ ſhal redouble yet ſhalbe worſe goodd myn ayde helpe ¶ whilis iaſon ſpack thus noble lady ſayde ſhe behelde hym ād right grete ardaunt loue ād coude abſteyne ſelf ſhe ſo ſurmounted loue time hyde wil refroide cole alityl without ſpeking jaſon ſhe left two damoiſelles entretene tarye hi ſhe withdrewe ito chā bre ſhe begā thinke grette vertues iaſon wete hye proweſſe fair chiere laughyng eyen well made body gracyouſe ſpeking ſo moche ſhe thought hym ſhe muſt come agayn vnto place then̄e ſhe fonude halle palays plente frendes moſt noble cyte ther newly artyued meſſager king damaſk certyfyed euenyng ſholde come vnto ayde ij thouſand aſſyriēs whiche king lord ſente conduyte hys broder named pruſiꝰ whiche right vaily āt knight armes theſe tydīges noble quene moche reconſorte 〈◊〉 ād commāded ſholde ordeyne wel hem ete drynke dide couere table receyued pruſius ryght ſolempnly whan eche ſette table fayr myrro ād iaſon ſuche wyſe woman one ny ••• ye may euery day haue new ther non̄ ſo grete playſir change ofte ha corfus ſayd then̄e king treu louer vſeth̄ neuer ſuche termes ye ſpeke whan prince may come loue lady fayr trewe diſcrete ād good houſe ynough̄ hym yf cometh̄ ſuche felicite goth̄ chaunge certes worthy reproche syre ſayde geant corfus ne knowe ye nomore then̄e ye ſaye ſhewe certes ther well another poynt ſayde king ſhall ſaye yow ſayde geant corfus take ye fayreſt lady liueth̄ amourous ouer euer ye may anone ye haue ēioyed lytill hit may ye ſhalbe wery full ſhe ſhall ſeme yow foule yet ſhal ſaye yow ſone yet ſhall wiſſhe brend yf ye men ye ſhall leue her▪ ād take yf hit puyſ •• unce • corfus ſaide then̄e king j ſhold beleue counceyll ſholde neuer well regarde j wene ie ſaie theſe thīge • ▪ make retorne coūtrey thende ye goo felde agaynſt yeſterday ſhedde bloode miloyaulte ſaid theūe corfus syre alle haue ſayd procedeth ony fere ne drede haue alle youre ennemyes counceylle yow trew power aſmoche ſemeth̄ hit couenable yowr helthe prouffyte thende youre wenyng founden vntre oute delaye ſhalle ſende meſſager vnto noble que ne myrro ſignefye mayntene noble meſtier armes offre ſelf alloū ayenſt viij beſte knightes ben cyte olyferne fyghte champe cloos hit apperteyneth ſuche caas whan kinge skla • onye herd āſuer geant perceyuid angry helde pee ſo long geant wēte armed hys tente ſyn put way ward cyte companye meſſager kinges ſente vnto quene myrro ryght ſuche wyſe fo ſayd whan meſſager ſaid change noble quene callid parte knightes declared geant demāded none olyferne herd contenue mandemēt moche iaſon plente knightes ſtraūgiers gaf honour ſpeke firſt ſame contre ſaye aduis werke say de alle hyhe geant corfus force vayllaūce put deth moſt part nobleſſe olyferne ſemed hit ſhold grete folye furmiſſhe bataylle demanded anſwere alle knightes ſtraungers ſo abaſſhed concluded cōd •• ted knightes oliferne reſeruid noble preu jaſon whiche might lē gher holde noble corage ſpeke ſayde wyth ſo hyhe voys wele vnderſtōde men manere hayr lordes diſpleſe yow vtue corage knowe febleſſe body j knowe rigght wel grete ne mē brrd geant neuertheles wel hit knowen ther geāt hath gretter hert then̄e hane ende appere euydētly noble lady herte wele reſteth̄ may alway goode tydinges j enterpryſe fyghte ayenſt geant corfus man man̄ ād j ſhall neuer reſte vnto time haue prou • ſelf ayenſt hym then̄e noble ladi quene tho preſent hauing herd thē terpriſe noble jaſō ſo vtterly ſmyten̄ ſorou ſemed ſhe ſmeten̄ ſpere trauers herte ſo moche ſhe louyd jaſon neuertheles ſhe helde goode contenan̄ce aſmoche paſſible incontinent iaſon hadde declared hys corage ſayde iaſō fayr ſire ware ye ſaye ſee yongthe abuſe yow yf ye xx armed point fyghte knowe ye knightes grece vnderſtode deſcended vytaille ſhippes ymagined anon̄ eſpyes hercules ſent theder teſpye roiaume wherfore renuoyed ſent agayn knight vnto grekes ād com̄anded thē ſtraytly diſpoſe diligēce departe lande go elli ſeke vytailles yf hadde nede yf departed ſodaynli diſancred toke ſom waye ſholde come puiſſaunce armes vpon ſo myghtily neuer ſholde haue wylle teſpie royaume cite caſtell ne countree whan jaſon felawſhip herd thexpreſſe rude commaūdemēt troyan king ſore diſpleſid withoute cauſe aſmoch muſte nedes departe noble jaſon better āſwerd curtoyſſy vnto knight ſhewed j ſory ye better cōtēt king lord hath receyued wyſe countree ye knowe wel curtoyſie ſhewid hit bleueth vnrecompē ſid ne rygour like wiſe hit remembrid ▪ moche meſfager j ſhal gladly make vnto king quene ād damoyſelles terrybly •• rifed loue theſe four knightes nether quene ne damoiſelle deſirid with̄ herte companye ſinguler eſpeciall beaute eche thē certes yſiphile thinſtaunt twoo noble eyē countree then̄e noble iaſon thinking demādes quene cōſidering grete daūger neceſſite famyne hunger ſurmoūted capiteyn chief vyage āſuerde hūbly ſayng manere madame pleſe hit yow knowe ben nōbre honderd knightes gentill men̄ one companye one coūtre bē departed one ſhippe haue vpon ſee ſo many infortunes tempeſte wīdes orages hath̄ holden v ſo long grete doubte periſſhid vytailles bē faylled v two dayes paſſid make ſhort goo ſeche vitailles helpe neceſſite syn hit pleſith̄ knowe frō coū tre bē parted whither attēde goo declare come grece ād oure entente ſalle ſo ferre til fiude yſſe ſee moche rycl • moton ſhepebering fleſe fyn golde • neuer knight yet powe ••• hardine • • quere ne approche nēyther beholde ſee many meruaillous terrible beſtes haue ī keping among • haue vnderſtande ther right cruell dragō wel haue allowed ꝓmiſed tauenture ſelfe cōquere hiter euer retorne agayn countre ſhall deye pourſuite therof many knightes haue don̄here fore wherof pyte ¶ wherfore right hye noble la dy requyre hūbly ye haue mercy pyte ād myn̄ infortunate felawes deyng diſtreſſe honger famyne maye haue vytailles four ſiluer moneye alſo grace ād leue remyſe make oure noble men̄ aſ oppynion ſholde grete ſynne ād meſfeet late thē deye famyne honger thēde • cludēd ſholde receyued theyr cyte notwihſtā ding ordenan̄ces ſtatutes bi fore made ſo moche • quene thei knew ſholde haue vytaylles paſſing yoyous ſemed propreli god deſcēded amōge thē thā cam fore ladyes whō thei ſale wed ryght reuerently ād anon quene ſawe noble cōpanye fore humilite ſhe deliuerid honderd lady honderd knightes grece eche one owne beſt ſemed ſhe reteyned jaſon part ſo moche grekes entred cyte ladyes oute difficulte brought thē theyr houſes eche departed frō eche lady feſted knight good viandes mete power ād good herte making chiere ſuch wiſe • facōn many knightes foūde hē ſo plainly grace ladyes aſmoch mighte ſerued termes loue ſaye thys tyme preſent continēt whan quene yſiphile ſawe ſhe jaſon • aillye ſhe ſomoche joyous ſhe might ſhe hadde ſette alle entēte beholde grete beaute noble prince aboue ſhe deſired haue acqueyntaūce beholdyng aduyſing hym ſhe made ſo many gracious ſignes tokenes loue many dayes often tymes noble iaſon whyche corage ſette place toke none hede ſhe myght lenger dure without ſhe ſholde ded ſomoch ſhe eſpryſed loue ād yet ſhe durſt ſpeke one word whan jaſon ſoiourned certayn ſpace nombre dayes ordeyned vnto hys patron̄moneye ſhippe might ſette inpoint ordeyned men ſholde helpe then̄e argo ſette hand vnto werk bi ryght alle knightes grece ād ī p̄ſence ſayde jaſō ſhippe mygt made agayn deꝑte thēs vin̄ monethes hole wherof many grekes meruayllouſly joyous whā hercules moche noble courage vnderſtode theſe tydinges noble quene myrro one daye ſette dyner jaſon iſiphile parceyued gracyouſe atrayns regardes ſhe gaf fte time vnto pren jaſon apperceyued right wel ſhe hadde ſette gyuē hym alle loue thus paſſed mele terribly amerous therfore j aduertiſe thē de ye finde menes ſpeke ꝑte yf ye may attyne therto yt ſhold right fayr paſſe temp ſpace alle ſholde fare better alle goddes anſwerd then̄e preu jaſon er preſente ben ſo diſpoſed enſie termes right renomed prince jaſon fore declared therfore counceyll ladyes gyue affiaūce ynowh doubting ſom wey abuſed thus ij gētil knightes ſpak fayr myrto yſiphile thisoroyſo • foloweth mar god ſufſraū ce god nature haſt puiſſaū ce chaūge nature beſtes thy propre vertue conduyteſt batailles ād bringest thē thy playſire thanke wyth alle herte thou haſt made doo praye humbly thou receyue ſacrefice ī gree thou wilt ꝯduyte myn honour ād bringe vnto countre thus whan thou haſt fyniſſhid thy prayer thou mayſt retourne glorye thy countre ſeaſed wyth noble f felte handes meruayllouſly ſofte ſemed herte hys body flewe ſo moche eſpryſed ardant deſir loue begā then̄e tenbraſe lady body ād syn behelde grete beaute thus doyng kyſſhed many tymes then̄e whan ben well eaſed waſſhed medea made lye bed heholdyng mē bres well formed ſhapen made hys colour fayr quyk coude tourne ſight thus beholdyng auyſing eche wyth oute ſayug ony word atte laſt noble preu jaſon toke worde ſayde dere lady ye knowe wel j haue promyſed huſbond also lyke wyſe ye haue promyſed wyf then̄e may ſaye youres ye ar myn̄ v two one thing then̄e requyre ſo • fe • tuelly may plaiſir ye may ye wylle come lye hete bed ha jaſon answerde then̄ inedea goddes ſake ſaue myn honour madaine āſwerde jaſo ther man world shal kepe then̄e j ſhal j houſbonde yf ye come lye bed ye doo nothīg honour dere frēde ſayde medea ther plaiſir shall gladly yow night ye ſhal haue pacyence requeſte praye yow morn̄ tyme ye deſire fadere king wolde gyue yon mariage then̄e ye deuoir cō tent ſhal make wedding ād ſpouſailles within honourably ſomone morn̄ nyght houre acuſtomed ād knowe ye certayn shal alle ye wille commāde reſon voū den therto vertue ꝓmeſſes made bytwene yow allewaye recommāde myn honour ¶ whan iason hadde vnderstande goode wille medea sayd corage ſhe wyſely anſwerd content tobeye requeſte shall saye night drew ouer ſuche termes sayd wel iason laye til day morn̄ whā ryſen sawe tyme made requeſte vnto noble king oetes wold gyue doughter medea mariage founde king oetes triſte moche penſif al wyſe then̄e acustomed made āſwere maner iason yebere yow oute dominacyon moſt ryche treſour ī alle worlde whiche greuith gretly yf hade knowen knowe ye comen tyme therto ād ye demāde doughter medea moſt con̄yng moſt dere thing haue suffiſe wy• ye haue neuer ſpeke therof alſo dere ye haue lyfe theſe ſemblable wordes king oetes wente oo ꝑt noble jaſon wente ſyde moche abaſſhed fiers ād herd anſwere hing oetes hercules theſeus mopſiuscam then̄e vnto iason whyche told hem howe bē wyth king oetes required haue hys wyf hys doughter medea howe kyng oetes hadde answerd fierſly whan vnderstanden alle thys concluded among wolde deꝑte thēs morn̄ don̄ wēt toke leue king thāked hym grete honour hit pleſid hym iason went viſited ſhip paſſid day litill plaiſir king oetes made hem chere notwithſtand whā night come iason wēte vnto fayr medea told made requeſte king oetes fader āſwerd regarde mariage deꝑted frō wherof fayr medea meruayllouſſy ſoroufull ſore troubled thinking many thinges whā ſhe wel bethought conſidering ca affaire ſhe made right goode chere jaſon ſhe abandon̄ed alle vnto plaiſir supposed night leye geder ſaye p̄ſent towching faites loue nyght fayr medea toke alle moſte richeſt jeweles bagges portatif king oetes fader ſhe putte truſſed fardell whan hit came alitill fore daye ſhe made jason ryſe whyche anon̄ redy then̄e whan ſhe alle redy ſhe toke alle rycheſſes alſo yong broder abſirthiꝰ aage xvj monethes whome ſhe toke secretly chambre nouryce made maistreſſe cutte hys throte pryuely certayn cause whiche shall declared fayr medea maiſtreſſe cladd hem ād diſgulſed mānes habyte noble preu jaſon brought vnto shippe aſſone jaſon deliuerid thē garde vnto maiſter maronner argo retourned chambre til day abyding felawſhip hercules theſeus mopſius many knightes cam hym blowing hor • ād toke flees goolde ſayde wolde departe then wyth alle dylygence certayn cauſes wythout ſayng thys tyme toke waye thende knightes grece ſholde folowe wente ſo ferre ētrid ī ſhip ſo well apoynt alle men entrid then̄e marō ners diſancred began rowe force oores aſinoche 〈◊〉 blewe winde helped hē cauſe hit calme thꝰ poynt putte waye vnto ſonne ryſing propre houre whā withdrawen past myle frō poorte hyt happend aduēture argo mayſter marōner began loke toward poorte ād sawe alle ſydes hit fulle peple ſawe anō apperceyueyd fowre lityll ſhippes facōn balingers orgaleyes ſubtyll departed gydre poorte whens came wherof good patrone argoshadde moch grete meruaille wiſte thenke ſo encombred he▪ hadde well ſeen whan noble preu iason hys companye entrid ſhippe king hys baron̄s ne ladyes conueyed hym grete meruaille ſayd one worde ¶ kyng oetes fader medea aduertiſed departing iason hys doughter medea folowed medea caſte broder abſirthyus piece ſee doubting fader kīg oetes howe noble quene yſiphyle fylle doun hyghe montayn̄ see demandeth thiſe foure litill galeyes ſnbtill cauſe moued fro port people inne hiſtorie anſwerth theyr entencyō come knightes grece king oetes one accompanyed foure honderd men whiche alle bourgeyſes toun̄ made armed ▪ aſmoche acertayned hys doughter medea goon̄ jaſon ſhalle telle kīg oetes ſaid ben ſorowful anoyed alle daye precedent fō de ſelf ſo full melancolye coude ſlepe ne reſte alleway many thoughtes precogitaciōs concluded hym ſelf wolde goo conueye iaſon departyng thys ende comen grece ſholde preyſe ād ſaye hadde made hī good chere brīge ēde cō cluſion aroos wyllyng ētre fro chambre chambre til cam jaſon entrid chambre nourice ſone abſirthius▪ fond wyth nourice ſlepte wherof ſore abaſſhid awaked nourire demanded wher hys dere ſone abſirthius then̄e nourire begā loke aboute nought ſhe fonde h • wherfore effrayed ſhe ſprāg bedde began ſeche diligētly alle aboutes kīg oetes entred chambre • medea ther fonde ne ꝑſone ne doughter ne gouerned long time ¶ whan king oetes fond doughter medea ſo angry blood changed ād withouthe ſpekyng ony worde wē te vp chābre noble iaſon logged fonde neyther jaſon ne medea ne ꝑſone might ſpeke ſo moche departed ſodainly wente vnto poorte fond many citezeins ſhewed ſhip grekes whiche time poorte then̄ quater myle then̄ kyng weping terderly demāded ſeen hys doughter medea anſwerde nay ha fayr ſirs ſayd then̄ king traictres grece haue wyhtdrawē wyt wordes traiterouſly ſomoche haue deceyued brought ſhip ād yet haue ſo euyll coūceylled ſhe hath born̄ ſone abſirthius euyl doughter euil fortuned child certes medea thy grete diſloyaulte ꝯſtrayneth wyth force peple j wil goo incōtinet fecche wete hath meuyd thus doo wyt ſhal take vengean̄ce deſloyall knight jaſon wiche power rē dreth euyl good ¶ whā king ſayd thus retorned palays cryēg euery man ſholde arme then̄e alle peple pourueyed ſtaue • armures ſyn demāded wherof proceded cauſe thys alarom̄e whiche anon̄ commune then̄e put • waye go vnto king whiche cam yſſued ont hys palays armed poynt tentre bataill then̄e wente vnto poorte cheſe four hōderd beſte po • put ſayd four galeyes finably whā • alle thys meuyd fro poorte ſayd wyth haſte made galeyes rowed knightes grece ſuche wyſe maiſter maronner apꝑceyued tho galeyes cam ſwiftely thē fecch agayn fayr medea called jaſon japed played wyth medea preſēt felawe hercules ſhe wid four galeyes armed wherein king oetes men wel poynt whyche approced faſte galeyes light jaſon ſeyng encombrance approche called hercules whyche knewe nothyng herof demanded counceyll then̄e hercules anſuerde hym knewe none remedie euery man ſhold putte armes redy tabyde batayll yf hit nede auowed vnto goddes yf king oetes made ony enterpryſe vpon thē wolde putte deth many mygh • arethe thiſe wordes wyth oute lē ger • aryeng noble knight hercules jaſon putte armes lyke wiſe dyde felawes then̄e medea maiſtreſſe ſprang vpon planck ſhyp beholde kyng galeyes anon̄ iaſon hercules alle ī armes cam vp hye medea eche wyth ſwerde fyſte medea began trē ble fere whā ſhe eſpyed fader approche ſo nyghe thēde king oetes pourſie wed ſore ſhippe noble preu jaſon force oores er goulf braas ſee nomore diſtance fro two bowe ſhote then̄ fayr medea ſeyng time brynge ende ſhe begon̄e fore ſayde maiſtres wepyng tenderly good mod wher lytyll broder abſirthius gyue then̄ euyll oolde woman opend lappe vnwonde body childe ſhe ſmytē piece medea toke heede lyſte hygh wherof hercules jaſon ſeyng grete horrour cruelte ād wereſore abaſſhed neuertheles whā preu iaſon apperceyued wold knowe fro • came thys creature ſo dede ſayde medea thys manere dere loue haue ye thought ye ſo malerous pyteus childe dere loue anſwerde then̄e medea thexperience werke enſeigneth yow thought herte madame anſwerde then̄e noble preu jaſon child ſee thus detrenched ſmyten piece certes euyll houre born̄ thus myſerabli hath finyſſhed hys dayes dere loue anſwerde then̄e fayr medea abſirthius yong broder knowe ye malerouſe ewrous happy thys daye ſhall cauſe ſauacion lyf fader men̄ then̄e moche ewrous goode oure born̄ whā hys tē dre yongth maye becauſe helthe ſo moche peple ād ſpecyally fader naturel certes medea ſaid then̄e jaſon ſee none facōn ne moyen ye poyntes diſhonoured whā ye haue cōmyſed ſo ryght pyetousa caas haue • rdryd ꝓpre broder innocent thinges hawhat horrible cruelte dere loue anſwerde then̄e medea ne troble wiſe then̄e reſō plaiſir ye ſhal ſhall ſaye ād caas make yow iuge ye know brought • fader ayēst wyll haue cōsiderid departyngis haue thoughte haue regarde vnto grete ād meruaillous courage fader al thing ouer thought conſiderid coude withdraw fer ſhold aduertiſed hath custome euery morenyng er goo doun̄ wil ſee sone ād alſo haue jmagyned anon̄ fyndeth ner ſone withonte faute wil come armes lyke ye ſee doth thus whan haue alle thiſe thinges considered grete daunger myght enſiewe v ſholde bataill mortall bytwene ād whiche withoute remedie ſhold ſlayn̄ takē hye vaylliaūce ſeen vnto de • h wold abandonne ſelfe recouuere thende teſchewe grete paryll dommage haue taken owen ſone broder ād haue cōmanded put hī ſtate ye ſee caſte tyme abrode ī cours ſee gyue empechement vnto ſhip fader whych then̄e ſhall tarye whā ſhalle ſee ſone abſirthius thus diſmēbrid flotyng vpon water garde recuyelle piece ye ſhall seen playnly anon̄ ¶ wyth thachieuemēt theſe deuiſes kīg oetes approched ſuche manere ſhippe grekes ther diſtan̄ce ſtone caste then̄e fayr medea olde woman fylled theyr hādes membris noble child abſirthius ſhewyng king oetes men̄ aſſone oolde quene ſspy • king ſhe eſcryed theſe wordes folowyng ād ſayd thus kyng wyſe come nere wenyng recouure thy ſone ne thy doughter regarde thy doughter thou loſeſt thy time ſhe maried vnto jaſō atte leſt ſhall rēdre thy ſone ſlayn ād detrēched piece whiche caſte ſee thēde thou maiſt haue thy lyf ſaued canſed haue occupacion recuyelle hys propre membres burye thē hit apperteyneth ſone kīg knowe thou thou ſholdeſt haue bataill ayēst knightes grece ben ſo hye vaylliaunces ther ne anymal monſtre ſerpent ne tyran̄t brynge deſtruc • yon then̄e hit ought bileuyd victorye bataill ſhold abyde wyth ād certes thou ſholdeſt receyue thy deth ſo alle thing well ouerſeē hit better thou retourne vnto cite then̄e tapproch ner receyue thy deth ād wel oughteſt thou haue grete yoye ſee thy happy ſone ded detrenched py • ce bi thy lyf reſpyted thou art ne naturell fader thou take hys membre • ſee thou ſo doo thy lyfe ſhall ſaued thy companye theſe wordes olde woman ād medea caſte ſee membres yong childe abſirthius kīg oetes hys peple heeryng ſeeyng grete inhumanite cruelte began eſcrye ryght pyetouſſy ād dolorouſ • ſo ſore vexed trobled thys meruailloꝰ auēture wiſt doo ſom ther begā wepe tenderli ſmote ſelf breſtes ſom began araye hem goo bataylle eſcryed deth knightes grece ſhoting thē arowes trait grete corage tanenge whan king ſawe • wyſe myght recouure deth hys dere ſone made ceſſe eſcarumſſij ſayd cytezels certes fair ſiresj pray trauaile nomore recouure medea ſhehath murdrid ꝓpre brod abſirthiꝰ whiche ſone • time come ſholde haue bē naturell lord certes j haue louid wyt herte alle lyfe wyt diſſoyall hath brouht one ſo dolorouſe guerdon̄ reward ha meda ſaid kīg hyghe j ſhal neuer ſech ne deſire mete wyt cauſe ſo cruell diſnaturell dede that▪ thou haſt • ſed thy propre blode therfore fay • lordes late ād alle ben goo goddes ſuffre hī knowe ye certayn yf j liberte ſholde make deye cruell deth howe wele ſholde ſourdre therof new ſorowe wherfore hit better ſhe goo entēde reaſſemble mēbres ſone whyche flotē ye may see vpō wawes ſee thende fleſſhe paſture byrdes ¶ whā then̄e noble bourgeyſes cyte vnderſtod king alle began ſech membres abſirthius iudemenyng moſte grete ſorow world ād thꝰ diſpoſed complaire kyng nomore taſſayle ennemyes whan fyſſhed membres child retorād vnto cyte ſpace tyme right ſorowfull diſconforted deth abſirthiꝰ aſmoche medea alſo goon̄ jaſon medea then̄e well ioyous ād aſſured then̄ fore whan ſhe apperceyuid fader mē taried fiſſhe mēbres ſone certes jaſon ſeyng ſayd wiſt thinke ād argo goode maronner rowed alle way withdrawing poorte ād yle colchos moche myght ſo moche alytil loſt ſighte king oetes galeyes ād cam hyhe ſee wind blewe arooſe anon̄ deſployed ſayle wōde • vp hyghe wherfore ſhippe made good way wherof argo moche yoyous then̄e ſayd euery man myghte leye doun̄ harnoys frely promyſing oute paril • time iaſon tyme ryght penſyf cruelte inhumanyte ſeen daye ſpak one worde ſemed cōpariſon̄ triſte then̄e joyous withoute cauſe whan medea vnderſtande argo aſſewryd alle companye tyme frō alle parils ben thoo conforted gretly ſhe behelde handes yet foule blood brother abſuthius ſhe wente waſſhed hem ād made hem clene ſhe cā ſette doun̄ iaſon seyng moche penſyf ſayde hī gracious curtays manere dere loue wheron thinke certes jaſon anſwerde one worde whan ſhe ſawe ſhe ſayde hī agayn ſame word dere loue jaſon wheron thinke yow then̄ iaſon anſwerde thus lady ſyn ye deſire knowe wheron thinke knowe ye trouth yf grete loue haue yow haue promyſed wed yow bryng yow grece wolde wherfore kepe henſſorward ye ſuche thing dere ye haue pee bytwene yow ād vpon thiſe wordes medea excuſed faireſt wyſe ſhe coude ād poſſible sayng alle ſhe veray good wille ſomoche ſhe ſo doyng ſuppoſed haue vſed cruelte ne humanyte ne hayne hate precedent ād nyght tofore goddeſſe deane ſhewed made reuelacyon king octes muſt nedes dey abſirthius ſone ſuche wordes colourīg caas ſhe traueyled ſo ſore ſhe foūde ſelf godod grace jaſon duryng thys voyage whan bē certain dayes ſee mopſius cam time iaſon theū brought remembran̄ce hou ꝓmyſed yſipſ • loued hym ſhe wayled frō morn̄ vnto euen vpon roche ſind ofte time thiſe propre wordes folowe ha neptunus god ſee windes dere loue jaſon bring agayn rendre hym agayn daye ād nyght wepeth lygheth hym ded alyue haue hym ipraye yow ye ſende grace ewer leuer day then̄e morn̄ thus then̄e ſhe alle diſcōforted one daye among alle ſhe loked ſee toward ceſt ſaw frō ferre ſhip moche deſired ſayled grete radour fulle ſaill jaſon certes ſhe knew anone well gretenes baners enſeignes diſplayed wyth winde wherof ſhe ſo grete gladneſſe ſhe begā make beſt chere worlde ſhe thus rauyſſhed grete ioye ād ſemed jaſon cā ſeuerly vnto wyth olde maiſtreſſe fayr medea putte ſorceries werke ād theire ēchātemēts wherof thauē ture ſhippe ſorted ſayd ſhe tourned al ſodainly coſte▪ wherof poure jſiphile abaſſhed ſore eſmayed ſtede make yoye ſhe conſtrayned wepe grete teeres ſtede ſyngyng ſhe enforced complayne ſhall ſaye ſodaynli ſhip torned ſo ſodaynly chaūged maner yſiphi le ſhe abode paſſed night propre herte ¶ wan ſixe wekes paſt ād fayr jſiphyle apꝑceyued ſhe ſholde haue tydinges loue iaſon thenchantemētes medea maiſtreſſe made ſhyppe iaſon mighte approche yle lennos ryght diſcōforted iſiphile ſeeyng ſayd vpon poynt full deſpayr ſhe departed • roche ſhe ben long abydyng meruaillous opynyō ſhe retorned lennos then̄e mhan ſhe entred chambre ſhe made ſone brought ſhe kyſſed many tymes loue iaſon began thinke contrepeyſe mynde ī diuerce maners then̄e whā ſhe long thought grete habōdā ce melancolye ſhe ſayde beholding child croſſing armes ſighe comyng borō hert ala dere ſone ala thou cāſt not▪ ſpeke demā de tydinges thy fader whyche mooſt fayre knight mooſt vertuous moſt vaylliaunt armes godd euer fourmed thou coudeſt ſpeke demande might wele anſwere ala wote neuer al auēture daygneth come auenture whā weneth come daie ſemed whā j knewe ſhippe whō wind tempeſt cōſtrained retorne ād ſayle thoppoſite ſhewīg bak trauerſing wawes flothes ſee ſo • petuouſ • j thīke better isperiſſhed then̄ fourty dayes j haue ſyn ſoyourned roche j ne coude neuer ſee wherof j right diſplaiſant herte dere ſone then̄e nature whiche ſholde enſeigne wepe then̄e loſſe one ſo deſired prince ought j deſire lyue may auaylle lyue certes ſholde lyue lyf ſholde hēs forth full cōtynuell bewaylinges dolour wepinges ſighes ſorow wote nomore ſaie haue ſomoche loued jaſon ꝑdurably conſtrayned wepe alle way creature ne deſire lyue enioye worldly plaiſan̄ces then̄e whan alle mondayn pleyſir faylleth ought j deſire j lyf certes nay then̄ hyt lyf lyueth deyeng deth lyueth languiſſhinge meruaillous right terrible deſire j ſhall deye verayly thys yourneye hit concluded ſom̄e euer ſhall may come therof j ſhall ſprī ge hye ſee thende noble preu jaſon buryed j may wyth caſte fyre ād venym owt throtes ſuche wyſe ſhe made toldye kyng quene hys doughter ſytting table conſequently al thē halle well yet mighte deporte thinke ineſtimnble beaute ād yet doo alle felawes aſſaylled hī agaymād caſte ſtones glayues ſwerdes wherwyt bruyſed wounded many place horions ſtrokes cam aboue neuertheles iaſon vaylliaunt knyght marchyd owt ouer paſſage dyde ſomoch cam right fayr lande then̄ brutorus folke ſiewed ſo ferre cam fyght hād hand among alle brutorus approched vnto euyll auē ture jaſon ſmote vpon toppe helme bi ſuch fierſte clefte helme heed vnto teeth fille doun̄ ded fete thus ye may vnderſtande diſloyall brutorꝰ miſerably flayn̄ then̄e whan companye apperceyued put vtteran̄ce eſcryed al vpon jaſon ād aſſayled new right anguiſſhouly renewyng hī dolour grete payne woundes ād frouſſhures made hym holowe waye ſayd ſo began ſtoure aſpre ād terryble well jaſon corage then̄e puiſſaunce alway defended hym right grete vigour bathing trenchaūt
